    <script id="search_results_item_tags" type="text/tmpl">
     &lt;%
        var title = '';
        var result_class = '';

        // If tag.is_query, we manufactured this tag in the client
        // It's the current search term in the search field
        // and that term did not return an exact match from the typeahead results
        // so we're prepending it to the result set on the fly
        if (tag.is_query) {
            title = '&lt;u&gt;' + tag.tag + '&lt;/u&gt;';
        } else {
            // Some tags don't match the substring and tag.hilite_tag doesn't get set
            // This ifalls back to the plain escaped tag.
            title = tag.hilite_tag || tag.escaped_tag;
        }

        if(!tag.featured &amp;&amp; !tag.unread_count) result_class += ' no_count';
        if(tag.thumb) result_class += ' has_thumb';
        if(tag.is_query) result_class += ' is_query';
        if(tag.is_featured) result_class += ' is_featured';

        tag.url = tag.url.replace('/tagged/', '/search/');

        // Skip results that don't have a title
        // because they look broken
        if (!title.length) return;

            <div class="post_content_inner">
             <div class="post_title">
              Based on Hawkeye having a farm
             </div>
             <div class="post_body" data-subview="body">
              <p>
               Steve: hey nat when you get this we are meeting up at clints farm. Ultron kinda scattered us so we shall regroup there. Need the address?
               <br/>
               Natasha: nope, i know where it is :)
               <br/>
               Steve: ok. be sure to bring a change of clothes, we might be here for a while.
               <br/>
               Natasha: ill be okay
               <br/>
               The avengers arrive at the farm to find the bathroom full of hair products and perfumes and Nats clothes everywhere. Tony picks up a bra from the couch and looks at Clint.
               <br/>
               Tony: i always took you for a b cup. Do you have the matching bottoms on?
               <br/>
               Nat walks in from behind them all and grabs it.
               <br/>
               Natasha: no, i do. Thanks, ive been looking for this. She looks at Clint. Barton, are the bedrooms clean? We dont want our friends to find any of your arrows.
               <br/>
               Steve: are we talking about
               <br/>
               Natasha: or any of mine she winks
               <br/>
               Steve: OKAY IM GONNA GO CHOP SOME WOOD
               <br/>
               Tony: Ill help
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>

            <div class="post_content_inner">
             <div class="post_title">
              True Love Pt. 2 (Pietro x Reader)
             </div>
             <div class="post_body" data-subview="body">
              <p>
               <b>
                <a href="http://pietroimagines.tumblr.com/post/123133087483/true-love-pietro-x-reader">
                 Part 1
                </a>
               </b>
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                Summary:
               </b>
               Pietro is debating whether or not he has a chance with you and if he should ditch his easy player life style and try his hardest to win your heart, or if he should forget about trying to pursue you and stay a player. Everything becomes clear to him after a trip to Clints farm with you and the team.
              </p>
              <p>
               <b>
                Warnings:
               </b>
               Smut in the beginning but the rest is just fluff. The smut scene is in between theKeep Reading and the first horizontal line so if you dont want to read the smut in this fic but you just want to read the fluff you can scroll past the scene and enjoy the fluffiness :)
              </p>
              <p class="tmblr-truncated read_more_container">
               <a class="tmblr-truncated-link read_more" href="http://pietroimagines.tumblr.com/post/123687313423/true-love-pt-2-pietro-x-reader">
                Keep reading
               </a>
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </section>

           <section class="post_content" data-subview="content">
            <div class="post_media">
             <a class="link-button link-button--default no-thumbnail" href="http://archiveofourown.org/works/4189905/chapters/9463176" target="_blank">
              <div class="info-container">
               <div class="publisher-container">
                <div class="publisher">
                 archiveofourown.org
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="title">
                Family Interviews - Chapter 1 - tehchi - Daredevil (TV), The Avengers (Marvel Movies) [Archive of Our Own]
               </div>
               <div class="excerpt">
                An Archive of Our Own, a project of the Organization for Transformative Works
               </div>
               <div class="author">
                By Organization for Transformative Works
               </div>
              </div>
             </a>
             <div class="post_content_inner">
              <div class="post_body" data-subview="body">
               <p>
                In response to the following prompt:
               </p>
               <p>
                Matt/Happiness - AU - Matt gets Adopted as a Kid
               </p>
               <p>
                Exactly
 what it says. Matt gets adopted by a loving family who help him deal 
with/heal from all the recent emotional trauma in his young life. Id 
prefer this be after Stick leaves, so Matt does get a handle on his 
super-senses. So Matt would be around 11? 12?
               </p>
               <p>
                Who adopts him? I 
dunno. For ultimate happiness AU, perhaps its Foggys family somehow 
(maybe in this AU theyre not as poor as the show implies), so the two 
of them grow up together. Maybe its an unrelated family but Matt and 
Foggy meet at school. Maybe Matt actually makes OTHER FRIENDS growing up
 in a more supportive environment. Maybe he has awesome adopted 
siblings.
               </p>
               <p>
                Id be especially interested to see how/if Matt gets 
into crimefighting in this AU. I feel like hed still feel the pull to 
use his abilities somehow. But less fueled by all his bitter emotional 
baggage.
               </p>
               <p>
                <br/>
               </p>
               <figure class="tmblr-full" data-tumblr-attribution="ixviimmxiii:-xY2-fL5bYV8oFXeNUhy1w:ZR72ku14kiCzM">
                <img class="" src="https://38.media.tumblr.com/17fe6c9ae772e86b52a145a792d25989/tumblr_mzmulxxkMN1rbgo35o1_500.gif"/>

           <section class="post_content" data-subview="content">
            <div class="post_content_inner">
             <div class="note_item">
              <div class="text">
               <p class="asker">
                <a class="name" href="http://frumiousme.tumblr.com/">
                 frumiousme
                </a>
                <span>
                 asked:
                </span>
               </p>
               <p>
                hey sweet lady! i have a question for your nerdiness. at the end of ep 1 s 1 of shield, do they drop mike's kid off at hawkeye's farm? or is it just a random farm?
               </p>
              </div>
              <div class="nipple">
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="avatar">
              <a href="http://frumiousme.tumblr.com/">
               <img alt="" height="40" src="https://33.media.tumblr.com/avatar_320605ede679_96.png" width="40"/>
              </a>
             </div>
             <div class="post_body">
              <p>
               Hi love!
              </p>
              <p>
               No, its not the same place. Neither inin universe nor in real life.
              </p>
              <p>
               InAoSAce is taken to Mikes sister, Mindy.
              </p>
              <p>
               Locations IRL:
              </p>
              <figure class="tmblr-full">
               <img class="" src="https://41.media.tumblr.com/9b8fe95bfac6d531cb4a3f836fb60af6/tumblr_inline_nrfarvWumI1sps28a_540.jpg"/>
              </figure>
              <p>
               Hawkeyes propertydoes not exist, It was a facade built in
               <a href="https://www.google.co.uk/maps/place/Stratfield+Saye+House/@51.348916,-0.995947,17z/data=!3m1!4b1!4m2!3m1!1s0x48769d97366975a1:0xd9bb6b1ce199ee17" target="_blank">
                Stratfield Saye
               </a>
               estate in Berkshire, the Duke of Wellingtons estate.
              </p>
              <figure class="tmblr-full">
               <img class="" src="https://41.media.tumblr.com/80ba53835e3357521aa007dc5d470ab4/tumblr_inline_nrfav3bSME1sps28a_540.jpg"/>
              </figure>
              <p>
               Aunt Mindys farm on the other hand is a real house, located at Ventura
Farms, at 555 W. Potrero Road, in Thousand Oaks, California.
              </p>
              <p>
               (sources:
               <a href="http://www.gamesradar.com/avengers-age-ultron-uk-locations-guide/" target="_blank">
                http://www.gamesradar.com/avengers-age-ultron-uk-locations-guide/
               </a>
              </p>
              <p>
               <a href="http://www.seeing-stars.com/Locations/SHIELD/index.shtml" target="_blank">
                http://www.seeing-stars.com/Locations/SHIELD/index.shtml
               </a>
               )
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>

data-post-id="124019101039" data-reblog-key="nT4x6Per" data-reblog_key="nT4x6Per" data-reblog_source="POST_CONTEXT_UNKOWN" data-root-id="124019101039" data-root_id="124019101039"            <section class="post_content" data-subview="content">
            <div class="post_content_inner">
             <div class="post_body" data-subview="body">
              <p>
               after comic con i had the sudden realization that i no longer give a flying fuck about the mcu and avengers (even the comics)
              </p>
              <p>
               like Im kind of done with those characters bc at this point the only ones i can tolerate are quicksilver (bc hes more of an xmen character), falcon, thor, and trash king hawkeye (not farm dad hawkeye)
              </p>
              <p>
               and like Im at the point where i know Im not going to pick up a single one of the avengers/avengers/mcu influenced books in October and Im not sure if thats out of spite for the disney-marvel brand or my overall distain for the fandom due to them putting the films and characters involved in them on such high pedestals
              </p>
              <p>
               then theres the whole inhumans mess, like honestly i want to see marvel get the rights back to the xmen just to see them fucking crash and burn sooooooooooo badly bc no one gives a shit about a group that literally has fucking slaves!!!!!!!!!!!!! like honestly i am so fucking done with that bc guess what marvel, the inhumans are not interesting characters and the only reason Im supporting ms. marvel is bc i know in a couple years when y'all realize what a shit idea the inhumans are theres going to be one big retcon around kamala bc y'all wont let her fall done with that sinking ship
              </p>
              <p>
               ugh Im just really frustrated with the mcu right now and like the only reason Im seeing ant man is bc my 12 year old brother wants me to take him after camp but like after that Im out
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </section>

@awwjeezTwitter - @Lukeusername","description_sanitized":"\u003Cp\u003ELuke William Thomas, a 20 year old Scriptwriting student at the University of Lincoln, falling around not knowing what I\u0027m doing\u003C\/p\u003E\u003Cp\u003EInstagram - @awwjeez\u003C\/p\u003E\u003Cp\u003ETwitter - @Lukeusername\u003C\/p\u003E","title":"Delicious Nose Clams","likes":true,"is_private":false,"is_group":false,"customizable":false,"following":false,"premium_partner":false},"tumblelog-parent-data":false,"tumblelog-root-data":false,"form-key":"!1231436915604|8PQscSpbxkIQ4L1F0eNmGVgKUI","form_key":"!1231436915604|8PQscSpbxkIQ4L1F0eNmGVgKUI","reblog_key":"mfHPL3zy","is_mine":false,"accepts_answers":false,"following_tumblelog":false,"liked":false,"sponsored":"","premium_tracked":null,"is_recommended":false,"placement_id":null,"featured_tags":[],"reblog_source":"POST_CONTEXT_UNKOWN","share_popover_data":{"tumblelog_name":"withnailian","embed_key":"4Y5SorSOkJLAx2HpYv8pzg","embed_did":"68b3f7c1ee5166d706139f68a0df7f1f59afd6db","post_id":"123895802646","root_id":"123895802646","post_url":"http:\/\/withnailian.tumblr.com\/post\/123895802646\/i-think-with-the-incredible-influx-of-superhero","post_tiny_url":"http:\/\/tmblr.co\/ZpW3gs1pOm_iM","is_private":0,"has_user":false,"has_facebook":false,"twitter_username":"","permalink_label":"Permalink","show_reporting_links":false,"abuse_url":"https:\/\/www.tumblr.com\/abuse","show_pinterest":false,"pinterest_share_window":"","show_flagging":true},"post-id":"123895802646","root-id":"123895802646","tumblelog-name":"withnailian","tumblelog-key":"tjTi5ZEHX","reblog-key":"mfHPL3zy","direct-video":"","featured-tags":"","following-tumblelog":false,"is-animated":false,"is-recommended":"","accepts-answers":"","serve-id":"UUPd3DipxeLCMx3paiIu","impression-url":null,"placement-id":""}' data-post-id="123895802646" data-reblog-key="mfHPL3zy" data-reblog_key="mfHPL3zy" data-reblog_source="POST_CONTEXT_UNKOWN" data-root-id="123895802646" data-root_id="123895802646" data-serve-id="UUPd3DipxeLCMx3paiIu" data-tumblelog="withnailian" data-tumblelog-key="tjTi5ZEHX" data-tumblelog-name="withnailian" data-tumblelog_key="tjTi5ZEHX" data-type="regular">
           <section class="post_content" data-subview="content">
            <div class="post_content_inner">
             <div class="post_body" data-subview="body">
              <p>
               I think with the incredible influx of superhero films that will be released in the next few years there needs to be something of a change in the way the human side of the story is told, particularly in elements like romance, guilt and God complexes. Age of Ultron was a great film but it was let down quite a lot by the lacking human elements like Hawkeyes farm and the sudden romance between the Hulk and Black Widow. These character elements need to start being explored in the narrative organically, just as much as their superhero origins. If all of the future films explore the human sides of their characters as much as the super parts in this way and the films evolve some what then the next few years should be incredibly interesting in film
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </section>
